ANIMATION\\\\\\\\_DURATION = 1; // seconds\\\\nconst ANIMATION\\\\\\\\_EASING = \\\\"expo.out\\\\";\\\\nconst ROW\\\\\\\\_DELAY = 75; // ms\\\\n// --- helpers ---\\\\nfunction extractImgUrl(el) {\\\\nif (!el) return \\\\"\\\\";\\\\n// If it\\\'s an <img>, prefer currentSrc (handles srcset), then src\\\\nif (el.tagName && el.tagName.toLowerCase() === \\\\"img\\\\") {\\\\nreturn (el.currentSrc || el.src || \\\\"\\\\").trim();\\\\n}\\\\n// If it\\\'s a div with bg-image\\\\nconst bg = getComputedStyle(el).backgroundImage || \\\\"\\\\";\\\\nconst match = bg.match(/url\\\\\\\\(([\\\'\\\\"]?)(.\\\\\\\\*?)\\\\\\\\1\\\\\\\\)/);\\\\nreturn match ? match[2] : \\\\"\\\\";\\\\n}\\\\nfunction uniq(arr) {\\\\nreturn [...new Set(arr)];\\\\n}\\\\nfunction initClientLogosScroll() {\\\\n// Scope to the component (optional, keeps things tidy if there are multiple)\\\\nconst clientsComponent = document.querySelector(\\\\".clients--component\\\\") || document;\\\\n// 1) Gather all SOURCE logos from CMS via attribute\\\\nconst sourceNodes = clientsComponent.querySelectorAll(\\\\"[clients-logos-src]\\\\");\\\\nconst logoSources = uniq(\\\\nArray.from(sourceNodes)\\\\n.map(extractImgUrl)\\\\n.filter((u) => u && !u.endsWith(\\\\"/\\\\"))\\\\n);\\\\nif (!logoSources.length) {\\\\nconsole.error(\\\\"No logo sources found via [clients-logos-src].\\\\");\\\\nreturn;\\\\n}\\\\n// 2) Find the visible list\\\\nconst clientsList = clientsComponent.querySelector(\\\\".clients--list\\\\");\\\\nif (!clientsList) {\\\\nconsole.error(\\\\"Clients list not found (.clients--list).\\\\");\\\\nreturn;\\\\n}\\\\ninitClientsList(clientsList, logoSources);\\\\n}\\\\nfunction initClientsList(clientsList, logoSources) {\\\\nconst clientItems = clientsList.querySelectorAll(\\\\".clients--item\\\\");\\\\nfunction getCurrentlyUsedLogos() {\\\\nconst allTargets = clientsList.querySelectorAll(\\\\"[clients-logos-target]\\\\");\\\\nreturn Array.from(allTargets)\\\\n.map((img) => img.getAttribute(\\\\"src\\\\") || \\\\"\\\\")\\\\n.filter(Boolean);\\\\n}\\\\nfunction getRandomUniqueLogos(count, exclude = []) {\\\\nconst available = logoSources.filter((src) => !exclude.includes(src));\\\\nconst pool = available.length >= count ? available : logoSources;\\\\nconst shuffled = [...pool].sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);\\\\nreturn shuffled.slice(0, Math.min(count, pool.length));\\\\n}\\\\nfunction assignLogosToGroup(targetImgs, exclude = []) {\\\\nif (!targetImgs.length) return;\\\\nconst picks = getRandomUniqueLogos(targetImgs.length, exclude);\\\\ntargetImgs.forEach((img, i) => {\\\\nconst newSrc = picks[i % picks.length];\\\\nif (newSrc && newSrc !== img.getAttribute(\\\\"src\\\\")) {\\\\nimg.setAttribute(\\\\"src\\\\", newSrc);\\\\n// Optional: clear srcset to avoid browser swapping sources\\\\nimg.removeAttribute(\\\\"srcset\\\\");\\\\n}\\\\n});\\\\n}\\\\nfunction assignInitialLogos() {\\\\nclientItems.forEach((item) => {\\\\nconst wraps = item.querySelectorAll(\\\\".clients--logo-wrap\\\\");\\\\nwraps.forEach((wrap) => {\\\\nconst logoImgs = wrap.querySelectorAll(\\\\"[clients-logos-target]\\\\");\\\\nassignLogosToGroup(Array.from(logoImgs), getCurrentlyUsedLogos());\\\\n});\\\\n});\\\\n}\\\\n// Initial fill\\\\nassignInitialLogos();\\\\n// Animate rows\\\\nconst logoRows = clientsList.querySelectorAll(\\\\".clients--logo-row\\\\");\\\\nsetInterval(() => {\\\\nlogoRows.forEach((row, rowIndex) => {\\\\nsetTimeout(() => {\\\\nconst wraps = row.querySelectorAll(\\\\".clients--logo-wrap\\\\");\\\\nif (wraps.length < 2) return;\\\\nconst wrapHeight = wraps[0].offsetHeight;\\\\ngsap.to(wraps, {\\\\ny: `-=${wrapHeight}px`,\\\\nduration: ANIMATION\\\\\\\\_DURATION,\\\\nease: ANIMATION\\\\\\\\_EASING,\\\\nonComplete: () => {\\\\n// Move first wrap to end\\\\nconst firstWrap = wraps[0];\\\\nrow.appendChild(firstWrap);\\\\n// Reset Y for all wraps\\\\ngsap.set(row.querySelectorAll(\\\\".clients--logo-wrap\\\\"), { y: 0 });\\\\n// Refill the moved wrap with new logos\\\\nconst imgs = firstWrap.querySelectorAll(\\\\"[clients-logos-target]\\\\");\\\\nassignLogosToGroup(Array.from(imgs), getCurrentlyUsedLogos());\\\\n},\\\\n});\\\\n}, rowIndex \\\\\\\\* ROW\\\\\\\\_DELAY);\\\\n});\\\\n}, ANIMATION\\\\\\\\_INTERVAL);\\\\n}\\\\n// Run after images are resolved so currentSrc is set for Webflow responsive datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import Optional, Any\nfrom jose import JWTError, jwt\nfrom passlib.context import CryptContext\nfrom cryptography.fernet import Fernet\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.primitives import hashes\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.primitives.kdf.pbkdf2 import PBKDF2\nfrom cryptography.hazmat.backends import default_backend\nimport base64\nimport secrets\n\nfrom app.core.config import settings\n\n\n# Password hashing\npwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")\n\n\ndef verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:\n    """Verify a password against a hash"""\n    return pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)\n\n\ndef get_password_hash(password: str) -> str:\n    """Hash a password"""\n    return pwd_context.hash(password)\n\n\ndef create_access_token(data: dict, expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:\n    """Create JWT access token"""\n    to_encode = data.copy()\n    if expires_delta:\n        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta\n    else:\n        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)\n    \n    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "access"})\n    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)\n    return encoded_jwt\n\n\ndef create_refresh_token(data: dict) -> str:\n    """Create JWT refresh token"""\n    to_encode = data.copy()\n    expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)\n    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "refresh"})\n    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)\n    return encoded_jwt\n\n\ndef decode_token(token: str) -> Optional[dict]:\n    """Decode and verify JWT token"""\n    try:\n        payload = jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])\n        return payload\n    except JWTError:\n        return None\n\n\ndef generate_api_key() -> str:\n    """Generate a secure API key"""\n    return secrets.token_urlsafe(32)\n\n\nclass EncryptionManager:\n    """Manage encryption/decryption of sensitive data (API keys, credentials)"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, master_key: Optional[str] = None):\n        """Initialize with master key"""\n        if master_key is None:\n            master_key = settings.SECRET_KEY\n        \n        # Derive encryption key from master key\n        kdf = PBKDF2(\n            algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),\n            length=32,\n            salt=b\'itechsmart-ninja-salt\',  # In production, use unique salt per deployment\n            iterations=100000,\n            backend=default_backend()\n        )\n        key = base64.urlsafe_b64encode(kdf.derive(master_key.encode()))\n        self.cipher = Fernet(key)\n    \n    def encrypt(self, data: str) -> str:\n        """Encrypt string data"""\n        if not data:\n            return ""\n        encrypted = self.cipher.encrypt(data.encode())\n        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(encrypted).decode()\n    \n    def decrypt(self, encrypted_data: str) -> str:\n        """Decrypt string data"""\n        if not encrypted_data:\n            return ""\n        try:\n            decoded = base64.urlsafe_b64decode(encrypted_data.encode())\n            decrypted = self.cipher.decrypt(decoded)\n            return decrypted.decode()\n        except Exception:\n            return ""\n    \n    def encrypt_dict(self, data: dict) -> dict:\n        """Encrypt all string values in a dictionary"""\n        encrypted = {}\n        for key, value in data.items():\n            if isinstance(value, str):\n                encrypted[key] = self.encrypt(value)\n            else:\n                encrypted[key] = value\n        return encrypted\n    \n    def decrypt_dict(self, encrypted_data: dict) -> dict:\n        """Decrypt all string values in a dictionary"""\n        decrypted = {}\n        for key, value in encrypted_data.items():\n            if isinstance(value, str) and value:\n                decrypted[key] = self.decrypt(value)\n            else:\n                decrypted[key] = value\n        return decrypted\n\n\n# Global encryption manager instance\nencryption_manager = EncryptionManager()\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Gamification\n    points = Column(Integer, default=0)\n    level = Column(Integer, default=1)\n    achievements = Column(JSON, default=list)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())\n    last_login = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))\n    \n    # Relationships\n    tasks = relationship("Task", back_populates="user", cascade="all, delete-orphan")\n    api_keys = relationship("APIKey", back_populates="user", cascade="all, delete-orphan")\n    settings = relationship("UserSettings", back_populates="user", uselist=False, cascade="all, delete-orphan")\n\n\nclass APIKey(Base):\n    """API Keys for external services (encrypted)"""\n    __tablename__ = "api_keys"\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"), nullable=False)\n    provider = Column(String, nullable=False)  # openai, anthropic, google, etc.\n    key_name = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    encrypted_key = Column(Text, nullable=False)\n    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)\n    \n    # Usage tracking\n    usage_count = Column(Integer, default=0)\n    last_used = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())\n    \n    # Relationships\n    user = relationship("User", back_populates="api_keys")\n\n\nclass UserSettings(Base):\n    """User-specific settings"""\n    __tablename__ = "user_settings"\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"), unique=True, nullable=False)\n    \n    # AI Preferences\n    default_ai_provider = Column(String, default="openai")\n    default_model = Column(String, default="gpt-4")\n    temperature = Column(Float, default=0.7)\n    max_tokens = Column(Integer, default=4000)\n    \n    # Notification Preferences\n    email_notifications = Column(Boolean, default=True)\n    push_notifications = Column(Boolean, default=True)\n    \n    # UI Preferences\n    theme = Column(String, default="light")\n    language = Column(String, default="en")\n    \n    # Other settings\n    settings_json = Column(JSON, default=dict)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())\n    \n    # Relationships\n    user = relationship("User", back_populates="settings")\n\n\nclass Task(Base):\n    """Task/Job execution model"""\n    __tablename__ = "tasks"\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"), nullable=False)\n    \n    # Task details\n    title = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    task_type = Column(String)  # research, code, website, analysis, etc.\n    status = Column(Enum(TaskStatus), default=TaskStatus.PENDING)\n    \n    # Execution details\n    agent_type = Column(String)  # researcher, coder, writer, analyst, etc.\n    ai_provider = Column(String)\n    ai_model = Column(String)\n    \n    # Progress tracking\n    progress = Column(Integer, default=0)  # 0-100\n    current_step = Column(String)\n    total_steps = Column(Integer)\n    \n    # Input/Output\n    input_data = Column(JSON)\n    output_data = Column(JSON)\n    artifacts = Column(JSON, default=list)  # Generated files, URLs, etc.\n    \n    # Execution metadata\n    started_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))\n    completed_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))\n    execution_time = Column(Float)  # seconds\n    \n    # Error handling\n    error_message = Column(Text)\n    retry_count = Column(Integer, default=0)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), onupdate=func.now())\n    \n    # Relationships\n    user = relationship("User", back_populates="tasks")\n    steps = relationship("TaskStep", back_populates="task", cascade="all, delete-orphan")\n\n\nclass TaskStep(Base):\n    """Individual steps within a task"""\n    __tablename__ = "task_steps"\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    task_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("tasks.id"), nullable=False)\n    \n    step_number = Column(Integer, nullable=False)\n    step_name = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    status = Column(Enum(TaskStatus), default=TaskStatus.PENDING)\n    \n    # Step execution\n    agent_used = Column(String)\n    input_data = Column(JSON)\n    output_data = Column(JSON)\n    \n    # Timing\n    started_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))\n    completed_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True))\n    execution_time = Column(Float)\n    \n    # Error handling\n    error_message = Column(Text)\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at = Column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now())\n    \n    # Relationships\n    task = relationship("Task", back_populates="steps")\n\n\nclass Template(Base):\n    """Automation templates"""\n    __tablename__ = "templates"\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    \n    name = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    description = Column(Text)\n    category = Column(String)  # Default implementation - can be overridden\n        return [\n            {\n                "step": 1,\n                "action": "analyze_task",\n                "description": f"Analyze the task: {task.get(\'description\', \'\')}"\n            },\n            {\n                "step": 2,\n                "action": "execute_task",\n                "description": "Execute the main task"\n            },\n            {\n                "step": 3,\n                "action": "verify_results",\n                "description": "Verify and validate results"\n            }\n        ]\n    \n    async def verify(self, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:\n        """Verify the execution result"""\n        # Default implementation\n        return result.get("success", False)\n    \n    def log_execution(self, task: Dict[str, Any], result: Dict[str, Any]):\n        """Log execution for history tracking"""\n        self.execution_history.append({\n            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            "task": task,\n            "result": result,\n            "agent": self.name\n        })\n    \n    def get_capabilities(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get agent capabilities"""\n        return [\n            {\n                "name": cap.name,\n                "description": cap.description,\n                "required_tools": cap.required_tools\n            }\n            for cap in self.capabilities\n        ]\n    \n    async def self_correct(self, task: Dict[str, Any], error: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Attempt to self-correct after an error"""\n        logger.warning(f"{self.name} attempting self-correction after error: {error}")\n        \n        # Analyze the error and retry with modifications\n        corrected_task = task.copy()\n        corrected_task["retry"] = True\n        corrected_task["previous_error"] = error\n        \n        try:\n            return await self.execute(corrected_task)\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"{self.name} self-correction failed: {str(e)}")\n            return {\n                "success": False,\n                "error": f"Self-correction failed: {str(e)}",\n                "original_error": error\n            }\n    \n    def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get current agent status"""\n        return {\n            "name": self.name,\n            "description": self.description,\n            "ai_provider": self.ai_provider,\n            "capabilities": len(self.capabilities),\n            "executions": len(self.execution_history),\n            "last_execution": self.execution_history[-1] if self.execution_history else None\n        }\n\n\nclass AgentResponse:\n    """Standardized agent response"""\n    \n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        success: bool,\n        data: Any = None,\n        error: Optional[str] = None,\n        metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ):\n        self.success = success\n        self.data = data\n        self.error = error\n        self.metadata = metadata or {}\n        self.timestamp = datetime.utcnow()\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Convert to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            "success": self.success,\n            "data": self.data,\n            "error": self.error,\n            "metadata": self.metadata,\n            "timestamp": self.timestamp.isoformat()\n        }\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

           "type": "report",\n            "format": "markdown",\n            "agent": self.name\n        }\n    \n    async def _generate_article(self, task: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n f"""# {title}\n\n{self._generate_introduction(topic, tone)}\n\n## Understanding {topic}\n\n{self._generate_body_content(topic, tone)}\n\n## Key Takeaways\n\n{self._generate_takeaways(topic)}\n\n## Any]:\n        """Generate step-by-step tutorial"""\n        title = task.get("title", "Tutorial")\n        steps = task.get("steps", [])\n        \n        content = f"""# {title}\n\n## What You\'ll Learn\n\nIn this tutorial, you\'ll learn how to {title.lower()}.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n- Basic programming knowledge\n- Development environment setup\n\n## Tutorial Steps\n\n"""\n        \n        for i, step in enumerate(steps, 1):\n            content += f"""### Step {i}: {step.get(\'title\', f\'Step {i}\')}\n\n{step.get(\'description\', \'\')}\n\n```{step.get(\'language\', \'bash\')}\n{step.get(\'code\', \'\')}\n```\n\n**Expected Output:**\n\n```\n{step.get(\'output\', \'\')}\n```\n\n---\n\n"""\n        \n        content += """## Next Steps\n\nNow that you\'ve completed this tutorial, you can:\n\n1. Explore advanced features\n2. Build your own projects\n3. Share your learnings\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n- Official documentation\n- Community forums\n- Video tutorials\n"""\n        \n        return {\n            "success": True,\n            "content": content,\n            "type": "tutorial",\n            "format": "markdown",\n            "agent": self.name\n        }\n    \n    async def _generate_generic_content(self, task: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Generate generic content"""\n        title = task.get("title", "Document")\n        content_type = task.get("type", "document")\n        \n        content = f"""# {title}\n\nThis is a {content_type} about {title}.\n\n## Content\n\n[Content will be generated based on specific requirements]\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis concludes the {content_type}.\n"""\n        \n        return {\n            "success": True,\n            "content": content,\n            "type": content_type,\n            "format": "markdown",\n            "agent": self.name\n        }\n    \n    # Helper methods\n    \n    def _format_list(self, items: List[str]) -> str:\n        """Format list items"""\n        if not items:\n            return "- Feature 1\\n- Feature 2\\n- Feature 3"\n        return "\\n".join(f"- {item}" for item in items)\n    \n    def _format_parameters(self, params: List[Dict]) -> str:\n        """Format API parameters"""\n        if not params:\n            return "No parameters required."\n        \n        result = "| Name | Type | Required | Description |\\n"\n        result += "|------|------|----------|-------------|\\n"\n        \n        for param in params:\n            result += f"| {param.get(\'name\', \'\')} | {param.get(\'type\', \'\')} | {param.get(\'required\', \'No\')} | {param.get(\'description\', \'\')} |\\n"\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _generate_toc(self, sections: List[Dict]) -> str:\n        """Generate table of contents"""\n        if not sections:\n            return ""\n        \n        toc = ""\n        for i, section in enumerate(sections, 1):\n            title = section.get(\'title\', f\'Section {i}\')\n            anchor = title.lower().replace(\' \', \'-\')\n            toc += f"{i}. [{title}](#{anchor})\\n"\n        \n        return toc\n    \n    def _format_findings(self, findings: List[str]) -> str:\n        """Format findings"""\n        if not findings:\n            return "- Key finding 1\\n- Key finding 2\\n- Key finding 3"\n        return "\\n".join(f"- {finding}" for finding in findings)\n    \n    def _format_metrics(self, metrics: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        """Format metrics"""\n        if not metrics:\n            return "No metrics available."\n        \n        result = "| Metric | Value |\\n|--------|-------|\\n"\n        for key, value in metrics.items():\n            result += f"| {key} | {value} |\\n"\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _format_trends(self, trends: List[str]) -> str:\n        """Format trends"""\n        if not trends:\n            return "No trends identified."\n        return "\\n".join(f"- {trend}" for trend in trends)\n    \n    def _format_recommendations(self, recommendations: List[str]) -> str:\n        """Format recommendations"""\n        if not recommendations:\n            return "1. Continue monitoring\\n2. Implement improvements\\n3. Review regularly"\n        return "\\n".join(f"{i}. {rec}" for i, rec in enumerate(recommendations, 1))\n    \n    def _get_current_date(self) -> str:\n        """Get current date"""\n        from datetime import datetime\n        return datetime.now().strftime("%B %d, %Y")\n    \n    def _generate_introduction(self, topic: str, tone: str) -> str:\n        """Generate introduction"""\n        return f"In this article, we\'ll explore {topic} and its implications. " \\\n               f"Understanding {topic} is crucial for modern development practices."\n    \n    def _generate_body_content(self, topic: str, tone: str) -> str:\n        """Generate body content"""\n        return f"{topic} represents an important concept in software development. " \\\n               f"By understanding and applying these principles, developers can create " \\\n               f"more efficient and maintainable solutions."\n    \n    def _generate_takeaways(self, topic: str) -> str:\n        """Generate key takeaways"""\n        return f"- {topic} is essential for modern development\\n" \\\n               f"- Implementation requires careful planning\\n" \\\n               f"- Best practices should be followed\\n" \\\n               f"- Continuous learning is important"\n    \n    def _generate_conclusion(self, topic: str, tone: str) -> str:\n        """Generate conclusion"""\n        return f"In conclusion, {topic} plays a vital role in software development. " \\\n               f"By following the guidelines and best practices outlined in this article, " \\\n               f"you can effectively implement {topic} in your projects."\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

     return plan\n    \n    async def _plan_analysis_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any], plan: TaskPlan) -> TaskPlan:\n        """Plan a data analysis task"""\n        data = task.get("data", {})\n report", dependencies=[3])\n        \n        return plan\n    \n    async def _plan_debug_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any], plan: TaskPlan) -> TaskPlan:\n        """Plan a debugging task"""\n        error = task.get("error", {})\n        code = task.get("code", "")\n        \n        plan.add_step("debugger", "analyze", "Analyze error")\n        plan.add_step("debugger", "root_cause", "Identify root cause", dependencies=[1])\n        plan.add_step("debugger", "fix", "Generate fix", dependencies=[2])\n        plan.add_step("coder", "test", "Test the fix", dependencies=[3])\n        plan.add_step("writer", "document", "Document the fix", dependencies=[4])\n        \n        return plan\n    \n    async def _plan_documentation_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any], plan: TaskPlan) -> TaskPlan:\n        """Plan a documentation task"""\n        doc_type = task.get("doc_type", "readme")\n        \n        if task.get("code"):\n            plan.add_step("coder", "review", "Review code structure")\n            plan.add_step("writer", "document", f"Generate {doc_type}", dependencies=[1])\n        else:\n            plan.add_step("researcher", "search", "Research topic")\n            plan.add_step("writer", "document", f"Generate {doc_type}", dependencies=[1])\n        \n        return plan\n    \n    async def _plan_general_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any], plan: TaskPlan) -> TaskPlan:\n        """Plan a general task"""\n        description = task.get("description", "")\n        \n        # Analyze task to determine required agents\n        required_agents = self._analyze_task_requirements(description)\n        \n        step_num = 1\n        for agent_name, action in required_agents:\n            deps = [step_num - 1] if step_num > 1 else []\n            plan.add_step(agent_name, action, f"{action} for: {description}", dependencies=deps)\n            step_num += 1\n        \n        return plan\n    \n    def _analyze_task_requirements(self, description: str) -> List[tuple]:\n        """Analyze task to determine required agents"""\n        description_lower = description.lower()\n        agents = []\n        \n        # Check for research needs\n        if any(word in description_lower for word in ["research", "find", "search", "information"]):\n            agents.append(("researcher", "search"))\n        \n        # Check for coding needs\n        if any(word in description_lower for word in ["code", "program", "develop", "build", "create"]):\n            agents.append(("coder", "generate"))\n        \n        # Check for analysis needs\n        if any(word in description_lower for word in ["analyze", "data", "statistics", "metrics"]):\n            agents.append(("analyst", "analyze"))\n        \n        # Check for writing needs\n        if any(word in description_lower for word in ["write", "document", "report", "article"]):\n            agents.append(("writer", "document"))\n        \n        # Check for debugging needs\n        if any(word in description_lower for word in ["debug", "fix", "error", "bug"]):\n            agents.append(("debugger", "analyze"))\n        \n        # Default to researcher if no specific needs identified\n        if not agents:\n            agents.append(("researcher", "search"))\n            agents.append(("writer", "document"))\n        \n        return agents\n    \n    async def _execute_plan(self, plan: TaskPlan, progress_callback=None) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Execute a task plan"""\n        results = []\n        \n        while not plan.is_complete() and not plan.has_failed():\n            # Get next executable step\n            next_step = plan.get_next_step()\n            \n            if not next_step:\n                # No more executable steps (might be waiting for dependencies)\n                if not plan.is_complete():\n                    logger.error("No executable steps but plan not complete - deadlock detected")\n                    break\n                break\n            \n            # Execute step\n            step_result = await self._execute_step(next_step, plan)\n            results.append(step_result)\n            \n            # Update progress\n            if progress_callback:\n                await progress_callback({\n                    "task_id": plan.task_id,\n                    "progress": plan.get_progress(),\n                    "current_step": next_step["step_number"],\n                    "total_steps": len(plan.steps),\n                    "step_result": step_result\n                })\n        \n        # Compile final result\n        final_result = {\n            "success": plan.is_complete() and not plan.has_failed(),\n            "task_id": plan.task_id,\n            "description": plan.description,\n            "steps_completed": sum(1 for s in plan.steps if s["status"] == "completed"),\n            "total_steps": len(plan.steps),\n            "results": results,\n            "execution_time": (plan.completed_at - plan.started_at).total_seconds() if plan.completed_at else None,\n            "orchestrator": "MultiAgentOrchestrator"\n        }\n        \n        return final_result\n    \n    async def _execute_step(self, step: Dict[str, Any], plan: TaskPlan) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Execute a single step"""\n        step_number = step["step_number"]\n        agent_name = step["agent"]\n        action = step["action"]\n        \n        logger.info(f"Executing step {step_number}: {agent_name}.{action}")\n        \n        # Mark step as started\n        plan.mark_step_started(step_number)\n        \n        try:\n            # Get agent\n            agent = self.agents.get(agent_name)\n            if not agent:\n                raise ValueError(f"Agent not found: {agent_name}")\n            \n            # Prepare task for agent\n            agent_task = {\n                "type": action,\n                "description": step["description"],\n                "context": self._gather_context(step, plan)\n            }\n            \n            # Execute agent task\n            result = await agent.execute(agent_task)\n            \n            # Mark step as completed\n            plan.mark_step_completed(step_number, result)\n            \n            return {\n                "step": step_number,\n                "agent": agent_name,\n                "action": action,\n                "success": result.get("success", True),\n                "result": result\n            }\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Step {step_number} failed: {str(e)}")\n            plan.mark_step_failed(step_number, str(e))\n            \n            return {\n                "step": step_number,\n                "agent": agent_name,\n                "action": action,\n                "success": False,\n                "error": str(e)\n            }\n    \n    def _gather_context(self, step: Dict[str, Any], plan: TaskPlan) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Gather context from previous steps"""\n        context = {}\n        \n        # Get results from dependency steps\n        for dep_num in step["dependencies"]:\n            if 0 < dep_num <= len(plan.steps):\n                dep_step = plan.steps[dep_num - 1]\n                if dep_step["result"]:\n                    context[f"step_{dep_num}"] = dep_step["result"]\n        \n        return context\n    \n    def get_agent_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get status of all agents"""\n        return {\n            agent_name: agent.get_status()\n            for agent_name, agent in self.agents.items()\n        }\n    \n    def get_active_tasks(self) -> "progress": plan.get_progress(),\n                "status": plan.status,\n                "steps": len(plan.steps),\n                "started_at": plan.started_at.isoformat() if plan.started_at else None\n            }\n            for plan in self.active_tasks.values()\n        ]\n    \n    def get_task_details(self, task_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get detailed information about a task"""\n        plan = self.active_tasks.get(task_id)\n        \n        if not plan:\n            # Check completed tasks\n            for completed_plan in self.completed_tasks:\n                if completed_plan.task_id == task_id:\n                    plan = completed_plan\n                    break\n        \n        if not plan:\n            return None\n        \n        return {\n """Generate with automatic fallback"""\n        providers_to_try = [provider_name] if provider_name else self.fallback_order\n        \n        for prov_name in providers_to_try:\n            provider
